## Chronological information

### Timeline

* [13 BBY](/wiki/13_BBY "13 BBY") (Prologue)[[7]](#cite_note-Timelines-7)

### Series

*[Star Wars Anthology Series](/wiki/Star_Wars_Anthology_Series "Star Wars Anthology Series")*

### Preceded by

*[Solo: A Star Wars Story](/wiki/Solo:_A_Star_Wars_Story "Solo: A Star Wars Story")*

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Movie)

:   "*A rebellion built on hope.*"
:   ―Tagline[[1]](#cite_note-Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story-1)

***Rogue One: A Star Wars Story*** is a [2016](/wiki/2016 "2016") film directed by [Gareth Edwards](/wiki/Gareth_Edwards "Gareth Edwards") and produced by [Lucasfilm](/wiki/Lucasfilm "Lucasfilm") president [Kathleen Kennedy](/wiki/Kathleen_Kennedy "Kathleen Kennedy"), amongst many others. The screenplay, written by [Chris Weitz](/wiki/Chris_Weitz "Chris Weitz") and [Tony Gilroy](/wiki/Tony_Gilroy "Tony Gilroy"), is based on a story by [John Knoll](/wiki/John_Knoll "John Knoll") and [Gary Whitta](/wiki/Gary_Whitta "Gary Whitta"). The film's score is composed by [Michael Giacchino](/wiki/Michael_Giacchino "Michael Giacchino"), marking the first live-action film in the *[Star Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars "Star Wars")* [canon](/wiki/Canon "Canon") to not be scored by [John Williams](/wiki/John_Williams "John Williams"). It is the first installment of the *[Star Wars Anthology Series](/wiki/Star_Wars_Anthology_Series "Star Wars Anthology Series")*.

*Rogue One* stars [Felicity Jones](/wiki/Felicity_Jones "Felicity Jones"), [Diego Luna](/wiki/Diego_Luna "Diego Luna"), [Ben Mendelsohn](/wiki/Ben_Mendelsohn "Ben Mendelsohn"), [Riz Ahmed](/wiki/Riz_Ahmed "Riz Ahmed"), [Donnie Yen](/wiki/Donnie_Yen "Donnie Yen"), [Jiang Wen](/wiki/Jiang_Wen "Jiang Wen"), [Forest Whitaker](/wiki/Forest_Whitaker "Forest Whitaker"), [Mads Mikkelsen](/wiki/Mads_Mikkelsen "Mads Mikkelsen"), and [Alan Tudyk](/wiki/Alan_Tudyk "Alan Tudyk"). [Genevieve O'Reilly](/wiki/Genevieve_O%27Reilly "Genevieve O'Reilly") reprises her role as [Mon Mothma](/wiki/Mon_Mothma "Mon Mothma"), the [leader](/wiki/Chancellor_(Rebel_Alliance) "Chancellor (Rebel Alliance)") of the [Rebel Alliance](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic"); O'Reilly portrayed the character for [2005](/wiki/2005 "2005")'s [*Star Wars*: Episode III *Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith"), but her scenes were cut. The film also sees two actors from the films reprise their iconic roles: [James Earl Jones](/wiki/James_Earl_Jones "James Earl Jones") as the voice of [Darth Vader](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") (the character is portrayed by [Spencer Wilding](/wiki/Spencer_Wilding "Spencer Wilding") and [Daniel Naprous](/wiki/Daniel_Naprous "Daniel Naprous")); and [Anthony Daniels](/wiki/Anthony_Daniels "Anthony Daniels") as [C-3PO](/wiki/C-3PO "C-3PO").

The film, which began production in [August](/wiki/August "August") [2015](/wiki/2015 "2015"), is set between [*Star Wars*: Episode III *Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith") and [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"). It is set closer to the latter film and focuses on the [formation](/wiki/Rogue_One "Rogue One") of the [Rebel Alliance](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") and their efforts to [steal](/wiki/Battle_of_Scarif "Battle of Scarif") the [plans](/wiki/Death_Star_plans "Death Star plans") to the [Death Star](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station"), an event that was referenced in the opening crawl of *A New Hope*. [Jyn Erso](/wiki/Jyn_Erso "Jyn Erso"), played by Jones, and a group of other characters band together to steal the plans from the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"). Edwards has described the film as "a grounded, war-based movie, one in which normal people have to come together to fight the Empire as opposed to relying on the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") or [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force")".

## Publisher's summary[]

:   "*'A New Hope' is the story of a boy who grows up in a tranquil home and dreams of joining a war. What if we have the story of a girl who grows up in a war and dreams of returning to the tranquillity of home?*"
:   ―Gareth Edwards[[8]](#cite_note-NYT-8)

*From Lucasfilm comes the first of the Star Wars standalone films, "Rogue One: A Star Wars Story," an all-new epic adventure. In a time of conflict, a group of unlikely heroes band together on a mission to steal the plans to the Death Star, the Empire's ultimate weapon of destruction. This key event in the Star Wars timeline brings together ordinary people who choose to do extraordinary things, and in doing so, become part of something greater than themselves. In theaters December 2016*.[[9]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_SW.com-9)

## Plot summary[]

### Capture of Galen Erso[]

:   "*The work has stalled. I need you to come back.*"
:   ―Director Orson Callan Krennic[[1]](#cite_note-Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story-1)

 [![Krennic and his death troopers arrive on Lah'mu to capture Galen Erso.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/Erso_Krennic_Reunion_RO.png/revision/latest?cb=20170127060553) [![Krennic and his death troopers arrive on Lah'mu to capture Galen Erso.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/Erso_Krennic_Reunion_RO.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170127060553)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a6/Erso_Krennic_Reunion_RO.png/revision/latest?cb=20170127060553) 

Krennic and his death troopers arrive on Lah'mu to capture Galen Erso.

 

Approximately [six](/wiki/13_BBY "13 BBY") [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") after the [formation](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") of the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), [Imperial](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") Director [Orson Krennic](/wiki/Orson_Callan_Krennic "Orson Callan Krennic") and a [squad](/wiki/Squad "Squad") of [death troopers](/wiki/Death_trooper "Death trooper") land on the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Lah'mu](/wiki/Lah%27mu "Lah'mu")
and [forcibly recruit](/wiki/Capture_of_Galen_Erso "Capture of Galen Erso") [scientist](/wiki/Scientist "Scientist") [Galen Erso](/wiki/Galen_Walton_Erso "Galen Walton Erso") to complete his work on the [Death Star](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station"), a [battle station](/wiki/Battle_station "Battle station") the Empire hopes to be capable of destroying entire [planets](/wiki/Planet "Planet"). Galen's wife, [Lyra Erso](/wiki/Lyra_Erso "Lyra Erso"), is killed when she shoots and injures Krennic in an attempt to stop him from taking her husband. Their daughter, [Jyn Erso](/wiki/Jyn_Erso "Jyn Erso"), goes into hiding until [Saw Gerrera](/wiki/Saw_Gerrera "Saw Gerrera"), leader of the [Partisans](/wiki/Partisans "Partisans"), rescues her and takes her in.

### Jyn's imprisonment[]

[Thirteen years later](/wiki/1_BBY "1 BBY"), an adult Jyn Erso, under the alias of Liana Halik, has been imprisoned in a [Detention](/wiki/Imperial_Detention_Center_%26_Labor_Camp_LEG-817 "Imperial Detention Center & Labor Camp LEG-817") center on [Wobani](/wiki/Wobani "Wobani"), sharing a cell with [Oolin Musters](/wiki/Oolin_Musters "Oolin Musters").

### Mission to the Ring of Kafrene[]

:   "*A planet killer! That's what he called it.*"
:   ―Tivik to Cassian Andor[[1]](#cite_note-Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story-1)

 [![Cassian and Tivik discuss the "planet killer](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/MissiontoKafrene.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170609102340) [![Cassian and Tivik discuss the "planet killer](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/MissiontoKafrene.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170609102340)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/19/MissiontoKafrene.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170609102340) 

Cassian and Tivik discuss the "planet killer."

 

On the [Ring of Kafrene](/wiki/Ring_of_Kafrene "Ring of Kafrene") trading outpost in [section nine](/wiki/Section_nine "Section nine"), the [Rebel](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") [Intelligence](/wiki/Rebel_Alliance_Intelligence_Service "Rebel Alliance Intelligence Service") [officer](/wiki/Officer "Officer"), [Captain](/wiki/Captain "Captain") [Cassian Andor](/wiki/Cassian_Jeron_Andor "Cassian Jeron Andor"), meets with a contact, a man named [Tivik](/wiki/Tivik "Tivik"), who reveals that an Imperial cargo pilot defected from the Galactic Empire the day before and is telling people that they are making a weapon with the [Kyber crystals](/wiki/Kyber_crystal "Kyber crystal") from [Jedha](/wiki/Jedha "Jedha"). After persuasion from Andor, Tivik reveals that the weapon is a "planet killer" and that Rook is telling people that Galen Erso, an old friend of Saw Gerrera's, sent him. Andor escapes before he can be caught by Imperial [stormtroopers](/wiki/Stormtrooper "Stormtrooper").

### An urgent message[]

:   "*I need to speak to Saw Gerrera...*"
:   ―Bodhi Rook[[1]](#cite_note-Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story-1)

Having defected, Imperial pilot [Bodhi Rook](/wiki/Bodhi_Rook "Bodhi Rook") seeks out Saw, carrying an important message from Galen concerning the Empire's construction of an ultimate weapon. He finds Gerrera's hideout on Jedha but Gerrera's Partisan soldiers, including [Benthic](/wiki/Benthic "Benthic"), are distrustful of Rook's intentions and capture him. They bring him before Gerrera and though Bodhi pleads his case to the Partisan leader, Gerrera does not trust him either, fearing that he is being lured into a trap. To discover if Rook is being truthful or not, Gerrera subjects him to the torturous creature [Bor Gullet](/wiki/Bor_Gullet "Bor Gullet"), an experience which leads to a temporary loss of Bodhi's sanity.

### Freeing Jyn Erso[]

:   "*We're up against the clock here, girl, so if there's nothing to talk about, we'll just put you back where we found you.*"
:   ―Davits Draven[[1]](#cite_note-Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story-1)

 [![Jyn before the Alliance High Command](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/69/JynAlliance.png/revision/latest?cb=20171109231929) [![Jyn before the Alliance High Command](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/69/JynAlliance.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20171109231929)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/69/JynAlliance.png/revision/latest?cb=20171109231929) 

Jyn before the Alliance High Command

 

Jyn is [freed](/wiki/Liberation_of_Erso "Liberation of Erso") from Imperial captivity by [Extraction Team Bravo](/wiki/Extraction_Team_Bravo "Extraction Team Bravo") and brought before Rebel leaders including [Mon Mothma](/wiki/Mon_Mothma "Mon Mothma"), [Jan Dodonna](/wiki/Jan_Dodonna "Jan Dodonna"), [Bail Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa"), [Davits Draven](/wiki/Davits_Draven "Davits Draven"), and Andor. They convince her to help get them an audience with Saw, whom Jyn has not seen since he abandoned her years prior. Though the mission is presented to Jyn as one of extraction, Draven covertly orders Cassian to kill Galen so as to prevent the weapon from being completed. Jyn, along with Cassian and his reprogrammed Imperial droid [K-2SO](/wiki/K-2SO "K-2SO"), set off for the moon Jedha in a Rebel U-wing.

### When has become now[]

:   "*When has become now, Director Krennic.*"
:   ―Governor Tarkin[[1]](#cite_note-Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story-1)

 [![Tarkin warns Krennic that failure will not be tolerated.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/ff/TarkinAndKrennic.png/revision/latest?cb=20200512011722) [![Tarkin warns Krennic that failure will not be tolerated.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/ff/TarkinAndKrennic.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20200512011722)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/ff/TarkinAndKrennic.png/revision/latest?cb=20200512011722) 

Tarkin warns Krennic that failure will not be tolerated.

 

On the bridge of the [*Imperial I*-class Star Destroyer](/wiki/Imperial_I-class_Star_Destroyer "Imperial I-class Star Destroyer") *[Executrix](/wiki/Executrix "Executrix")*, [Governor](/wiki/Governor "Governor") [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin") monitors construction of the Death Star. As he looks on, the [superlaser](/wiki/Mk_I_Superlaser "Mk I Superlaser") is being installed. Krennic comes aboard the [Star Destroyer](/wiki/Star_Destroyer "Star Destroyer") and approaches Tarkin on the bridge. Tarkin expresses his concern over the defected [cargo pilot](/wiki/Bodhi_Rook "Bodhi Rook"), who is spreading rumors on [Jedha](/wiki/Jedha "Jedha") about the Death Star's existence. He tells Krennic that his time is up as far as completing the battle station goes and that [the Emperor](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") would not tolerate any more delays on the project. Suggesting that both problems should be solved together with a test of the weapon, Tarkin makes it clear to Krennic that failure will not be tolerated.

### Battle on Jedha[]

:   "*This town is ready to blow.*"
:   ―Cassian Jeron Andor[[1]](#cite_note-Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story-1)

 [![Chirrut engages stormtroopers during the Battle on Jedha.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/68/ChirrutImweStormtroopersJedha-R1.png/revision/latest?cb=20160813201653) [![Chirrut engages stormtroopers during the Battle on Jedha.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/68/ChirrutImweStormtroopersJedha-R1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20160813201653)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/68/ChirrutImweStormtroopersJedha-R1.png/revision/latest?cb=20160813201653) 

Chirrut engages stormtroopers during the Battle on Jedha.

 

Cassian, Jyn and K-2SO arrive on [Jedha](/wiki/Jedha "Jedha") where Cassian expects to meet up with a Partisan contact. The droid stays on the ship while Jyn and Cassian set out to find his contact, but the duo is caught in the middle of an armed uprising against the Empire led by Gerrera's partisans. Jyn and Cassian find safety only after K-2SO disobeys orders to stay on the U-Wing and comes to their aid. After fighting off the Imperial troopers, the convoy returns to [Tythoni Square](/wiki/Tythoni_Square "Tythoni Square") where the uprising had taken place. Imperial reinforcements arrive and K-2SO is mistaken for an actual Imperial droid transporting prisoners. The droid tries to play along, but the disguise is foiled. They are saved by the intervention of blind warrior [Chirrut Îmwe](/wiki/Chirrut_%C3%8Emwe "Chirrut Îmwe") and mercenary [Baze Malbus](/wiki/Baze_Malbus "Baze Malbus"), guardians of the Kyber Temple on Jedha, which the Empire is stripping of its treasures. After the Imperial reinforcements are fought off, the group thinks they are in the clear until a group of Partisans, including Benthic, arrives and takes over the square, kidnapping Andor, Erso, and the two guardians with K2 having gone back to the ship. Benthic feels that Andor was hostile towards the Partisans during the uprising because he shot one of their own who was preparing to throw a grenade at a tank next to which Jyn was hiding. Jyn reveals to the Partisans that she is the daughter of Galen Erso and the partisans take them to their headquarters in the [Catacombs of Cadera](/wiki/Catacombs_of_Cadera "Catacombs of Cadera") and imprison them.

### Galen's message[]

:   "*The reactor module, that's the key. That's the place I've laid my trap.*"
:   ―Galen Walton Erso[[1]](#cite_note-Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story-1)

 [![Galen's message revealing the Death Star's flaw.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/GalenErsoMessage-R1.png/revision/latest?cb=20171111050726) [![Galen's message revealing the Death Star's flaw.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/GalenErsoMessage-R1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20171111050726)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/7d/GalenErsoMessage-R1.png/revision/latest?cb=20171111050726) 

Galen's message revealing the Death Star's flaw.

 

While Cassian, Chirrut, and Baze are locked in cells, Jyn is brought before Saw. The calm captive Chirrut "prays" to the Force with his mantra "I am one with the Force and the Force is with me" while Baze mocks his partner's mystical ways. Cassian becomes impatient with Chirrut and begins to try and pick the cell lock himself. Gerrera is surprised to see Jyn, having parted ways with her years before. He is still wary that the pilot's message and Jyn's return is simply a trap but when Jyn explains her intentions of finding Galen he becomes more comfortable. He questions what Jyn wants to obtain from this to which Jyn answers that she wants no part of it and that her role is finished. Refusing to believe that Jyn no longer cares about the Rebel cause, Gerrera offers to show her something that he feels will change her mind. Meanwhile, on the Death Star, Tarkin and Krennic prepare to test the weapon on Jedha City, having evacuated all Imperial forces from the moon via [Protocol 13](/wiki/Protocol_13 "Protocol 13"). Krennic goes to order the complete destruction of the moon, but Tarkin overrules him and orders that the test-firing be conducted at minimum power. With imminent danger approaching, unbeknownst to those on the moon, Cassian, Chirrut, and Baze linger in their cells. They notice that in the cell next to them is an Imperial pilot, Bodhi Rook, and Cassian begins to question him, curious if he is the cargo pilot that brought the message. Bor Gullet's effects on Bodhi are clear and he does not seem to understand what Cassian is talking about until he mentions Galen's name and Rook's memory is jogged. As the Death Star's superweapon commences primary ignition above the moon, Gerrera begins to show Jyn the message that Bodhi brought. The message is a hologram, in which Jyn's father expresses his love for her and discloses his coerced help on the Death Star project. Galen also reveals that he covertly compromised the Death Star's design by including a subtle vulnerability in its reactor that can be used to destroy it. He tells her that the structural plans are at an Imperial high-security data bank on the planet Scarif. However, before the hologram can finish, the Death Star fires on the moon and chaos ensues.

### Destruction of Jedha City[]

:   "*Save the Rebellion! Save the dream!*"
:   ―Saw Gerrera[[1]](#cite_note-Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story-1)

 [![Saw Gerrera's fate is sealed.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/SawGerreraAcceptsFate-R1.png/revision/latest?cb=20171112193522) [![Saw Gerrera's fate is sealed.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/SawGerreraAcceptsFate-R1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20171112193522)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/SawGerreraAcceptsFate-R1.png/revision/latest?cb=20171112193522) 

Saw Gerrera's fate is sealed.

 

As the imminent destruction of Jedha City begins, the Partisans in the Catacombs begin to flee. Cassian quickly hot-wires the cell door and he, Chirrut, and Baze escape captivity. Cassian hurries to the convoy's possessions that were seized when the Partisans kidnapped them and frantically uses his comlink to call K-2SO who describes the destruction ensuing outside. Cassian informs him to locate their position so they can escape. Before they can flee, Cassian goes to find Jyn, telling Chirrut and Baze to free the pilot, which Baze does by blasting the cell door with his [MWC-35c "Staccato Lightning" repeating cannon](/wiki/MWC-35c_%22Staccato_Lightning%22_repeating_cannon "MWC-35c \"Staccato Lightning\" repeating cannon"). Cassian locates Jyn and informs her that Bodhi has told him where her father is. Gerrera urges her to go with Cassian, but when Jyn suggests he comes with them he refuses, electing to remain there and die with the city. The mass exodus of the catacombs begins, and those who exit look on in horror as they see Jedha's surface beginning to peel back, destroying everything in its path. As the Catacombs begin to collapse along with everything else, K-2SO pilots the U-wing through the destruction to pick up the convoy. Cassian, Jyn, Chirrut, Baze, and Bodhi hurriedly board the U-wing and the ship begins its escape through the destruction. Gerrera watches from the collapsing Catacombs as the U-wing takes off and the blast wave overtakes the area. Shortly before his impending death, Gerrera tears off his breath mask and accepts his fate. Jyn watches from the U-wing as the wave consumes the Catacombs and kills Gerrera. The convoy looks on in horror at the destruction outside as K-2SO and Cassian pilot the U-wing, fleeing the destruction that threatens to overtake them. Barely escaping the blast wave, Cassian hurriedly punches in the calculations and the U-wing blasts into hyperspace, narrowly escaping Jedha.

 [![Krennic and Tarkin look on as Jedha City is destroyed.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/67/Destruction_of_Jedha_City_Aftermath.png/revision/latest?cb=20171112025034) [![Krennic and Tarkin look on as Jedha City is destroyed.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/67/Destruction_of_Jedha_City_Aftermath.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20171112025034)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/67/Destruction_of_Jedha_City_Aftermath.png/revision/latest?cb=20171112025034) 

Krennic and Tarkin look on as Jedha City is destroyed.

 

As the Death Star's demonstration is carried out, Krennic, Tarkin, and many other Imperials look on. Krennic expresses the "beauty" of the destruction. With the demonstration complete, Tarkin congratulates Krennic but promptly uses Rook's defection from Galen Erso's Imperial facility on Eadu and the security leak on Jedha under Krennic's command as a pretext to take control over the project. Enraged, Krennic openly challenges Tarkin's decision and decides to deal with the defector and the potential Rebel sympathizer on Eadu personally. In the aftermath of the incident on Jedha, Cassian sends a coded message back to the Alliance base to inform them that Jedha has been destroyed and that he has learned that Galen is on Eadu. Receiving the message, General Draven is dumbfounded by the destruction of Jedha City but advises Andor to keep to the plan of killing Galen. Already in hyperspace, Cassian receives Draven's instructions and informs K-2SO to set their course for Eadu. The entire convoy is in shock concerning Jedha's destruction, and a troubled Chirrut begs Baze to describe the extent of the destruction. Baze reluctantly consents. Knowing now that her father is on Eadu, Jyn explains to Bodhi — who mistakenly believes that his message was too late — that Galen has laid a trap in the Death Star. However, with the message having been destroyed in the chaos on Jedha, she has no way of backing up her claims and the group is wary to believe her. With Cassian refusing to send word of Jyn's claim to the Alliance, she resolves to get her father on Eadu and bring him back to the Alliance so that he can tell them himself.

### Mission to Eadu[]

:   "*The Force moves darkly near a creature that is about to kill.*"
:   ―Chirrut Îmwe[[1]](#cite_note-Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story-1)

With Tarkin having seized control of the Death Star project, Krennic departs the Death Star in his [ST 149](/wiki/ST-149 "ST-149") shuttle en route for Eadu, where he plans to expose the Rebel sympathizer in Galen Erso's team. Meanwhile, the Rebel convoy, also seeking out Galen Erso on Eadu, approaches the planet in their U-wing. The planet's stormy conditions hinder their approach, and as Bodhi guides them towards the Imperial installation, they crash whilst attempting to avoid Imperial detection.

Jyn tracks her father to an Imperial research facility on the planet [Eadu](/wiki/Eadu "Eadu"), where Cassian chooses not to kill Galen. When Krennic arrives and threatens to have Galen's main team killed for causing the security leak, Galen confesses he is responsible. Krennic executes the team nevertheless, and Jyn makes her presence known just as a Rebel bombing raid begins, leaving Galen fatally wounded. Jyn's father dies in her arms before she and her group escape in a stolen Imperial cargo shuttle.

### Krennic's groveling on Mustafar[]

:   "*Be careful not to choke on your aspirations, Director.*"
:   ―Darth Vader to Orson Krennic — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/47/Vader-BeCareful.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250406161030)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:Vader-BeCareful.flac "File:Vader-BeCareful.flac"))[[1]](#cite_note-Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story-1)

 [![Vader confronts Krennic at Mustafar following the news of Galen Erso's betrayal](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/51/VaderAndKrennicOnMustafar.png/revision/latest?cb=20171112045158) [![Vader confronts Krennic at Mustafar following the news of Galen Erso's betrayal](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/51/VaderAndKrennicOnMustafar.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20171112045158)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/5/51/VaderAndKrennicOnMustafar.png/revision/latest?cb=20171112045158) 

Vader confronts Krennic at Mustafar following the news of Galen Erso's betrayal

 

With Galen Erso silenced, Krennic travels to [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar") to speak with the mysterious Dark Lord, [Darth Vader](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") at his castle. Upon Krennic's arrival, the Dark Lord's servant, [Vaneé](/wiki/Vane%C3%A9 "Vaneé") alerts Vader, who is meditating in a rejuvenation chamber, that the Director has arrived. Vader exits his meditation to confront Krennic on a platform overlooking the volcanic landscape of the planet. The Dark Lord expresses his concern that the Death Star has become more of a problem than the solution it was intended to be, citing Krennic's inability to keep the project a secret as the main catalyst for the change in approach. Krennic defends himself and his creation, claiming that he has delivered a remarkable weapon to the Emperor. Because of his self proclaimed success, he petitions that Vader grant him an opportunity to personally meet with the Emperor and advise him of the Death Star's unprecedented potential. Vader, however, is far more concerned about the rumors that had reached the higher levels of the Empire of the destruction of Jedha City and the attack on the Eadu facility by the Rebellion and what these revelations mean as far as the secrecy surrounding the Death Star project. Krennic attempts to shift blame onto Tarkin for having ordered the demonstration on Jedha, but Vader is not impressed by this futile effort and criticizes Krennic's groveling, reminding the Director that the secrecy behind the Death Star project was instituted in order to prevent open defiance from the Senate. Vader suggests that the Jedha incident be disguised as a mining disaster, but seems to imply that Galen Erso's betrayal might have been a bitter blow to the Empire's secrecy. Vader instructs Krennic to ensure that no other leaks occur so that the Emperor would be satisfied that the project had not been compromised. As Vader swiftly departs, Krennic makes a last plea for his continued control over the project, hoping to remain in command of the battle station rather than Tarkin. However, Vader's patience has run thin, and when Krennic requests that Vader speak to the Emperor on his behalf, the Dark Lord [chokes](/wiki/Force_choke "Force choke") the Director using [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force"). As Krennic falls to his knees, Vader warns him to temper his aspirations, lest they cause his downfall. He releases Krennic and the conversation is ended.

### Rebel council meeting[]

:   "*Rebellions are built on hope.*"
:   ―Jyn Erso[[1]](#cite_note-Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story-1)

 [![Jyn pleads to the Alliance High Command to take action on Scarif.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/JynBeforetheAllianceHighCommand.png/revision/latest?cb=20171112051939) [![Jyn pleads to the Alliance High Command to take action on Scarif.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/JynBeforetheAllianceHighCommand.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20171112051939)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/JynBeforetheAllianceHighCommand.png/revision/latest?cb=20171112051939) 

Jyn pleads to the Alliance High Command to take action on Scarif.

 

Having returned to the Rebel base on Yavin 4, Jyn and Bodhi are both present at an Alliance Council meeting where Jyn proposes for the rebels to travel to Scarif and steal the Death Star schematics so they will know where to target the flawed reactor module. The Rebel leadership — including Mon Mothma, Jan Dodonna, Bail Organa, [Tynnra Pamlo](/wiki/Tynnra_Pamlo "Tynnra Pamlo"), [Nower Jebel](/wiki/Nower_Jebel "Nower Jebel"), [Vasp Vaspar](/wiki/Vasp_Vaspar "Vasp Vaspar"), Davits Draven, [Admiral](/wiki/Admiral "Admiral") [Raddus](/wiki/Raddus "Raddus"), and [Antoc Merrick](/wiki/Antoc_Merrick "Antoc Merrick") — cannot come to a consensus; many of the Senators propose to scatter their fleet because they have no choice but to surrender. Mothma, Organa, and Raddus attempt to defend Jyn's plan. Unfortunately for them, with Galen Erso and Saw Gerrera dead, and their hologram destroyed, the Rebel leadership has no way of verifying Jyn's claims. The fearful opposition of Pamlo, Vaspar, and Jebel outweighs the support, despite an impassioned plea from Jyn, calling for hope. Without the full support of the council, Mothma is forced to play the devil's advocate, declaring the odds too great to commit so much of their forces.

### Rogue One departs for Scarif[]

:   "*Rogue One, pulling away.*"
:   ―Bodhi Rook[[1]](#cite_note-Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story-1)

Frustrated at their inaction, Jyn, Cassian, K-2SO, and a number of Rebels volunteer to take matters into their own hands. The party takes the shuttle to raid the databank themselves. Before they take off, however, they are confronted by Rebel command, who asks them to identify themselves. Rook improvises a call sign of "Rogue One" before heading off to Scarif without Alliance permission.

### The Battle of Scarif[]

:   "*They've no idea we're coming. They've no reason to expect us. If we can make it to the ground, we'll take the next chance, and the next, on and on until we win, or the chances are spent.*"
:   ―Jyn Erso to the members of Rogue One — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6f/Jyn-TakeTheNextChance.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250406160856)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:Jyn-TakeTheNextChance.flac "File:Jyn-TakeTheNextChance.flac"))[[1]](#cite_note-Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story-1)

Once Rogue One arrives at Scarif, they begin to transmit a clearance code, praying that it has not been listed as overdue. Fortunately, the code is valid. The team enters the [Shield Gate](/wiki/Shield_Gate "Shield Gate") and head to the planet below. Briefly, before starting the mission, Jyn speaks to the squad in an effort to inspire them, emphasizing that despite being clearly outnumbered, anything is possible with the element of surprise on their side. Cassian debriefs the men and orders them to attack the troops as a distraction so they can gain entry to the Citadel and find the plans. As Jyn, Cassian, and K-2SO search the data bank for the design plans, the rest of their team set off explosives and commence firing in the nearby landing area in an attempt to distract the resident stormtroopers.

Arriving at Scarif, Rogue One jumps the inspection team and steals their uniforms. Jyn and Cassian masquerade as the inspection team and gain entrance to the Citadel with K-2SO in tow.

Inside the Citadel, K-2SO hacks into another Imperial droid of the same model to gain intelligence to locate and access the vault. Krennic orders the [garrison](/wiki/Scarif_Deployment "Scarif Deployment") deployed after the squad sets off the diversionary explosives. Tarkin is alerted that the Scarif installation has been compromised by rebels and is concerned the rebels may be after the Death Star plans. Tarkin has Lord Vader informed of the developments before ordering the Death Star into hyperspace to investigate.

Meanwhile, back at the Rebel headquarters on Yavin 4, the Rebellion learn of the battle from intercepted Imperial transmissions but before the council is notified, Admiral Raddus has already sent his fleet in support of Rogue One's efforts.

While Rogue One is battling the stormtroopers, Bodhi contacts Scarif Imperial headquarters and feeds them false information and create confusion in order to give the squad a better tactical advantage. The garrison deploys [AT-ACT](/wiki/All_Terrain_Armored_Cargo_Transport "All Terrain Armored Cargo Transport") walkers to battle the squad.

Once Raddus's fleet arrives, [Red](/wiki/Red_Squadron_(Rebel_Alliance) "Red Squadron (Rebel Alliance)") and [Gold Squadrons](/wiki/Gold_Squadron_(Rebel_Alliance) "Gold Squadron (Rebel Alliance)") are ordered to protect the fleet, while [Blue](/wiki/Blue_Squadron_(Rebel_Alliance) "Blue Squadron (Rebel Alliance)") Squadron is ordered to get to the surface to reinforce and provide air support to Rogue One battling on the beaches. Several X-wings, including Blue Leader [Antoc Merrick](/wiki/Antoc_Merrick "Antoc Merrick"), and a single [U-wing](/wiki/UT-60D_U-wing_starfighter/support_craft "UT-60D U-wing starfighter/support craft") gunship make it through the opening before [Gate Control](/wiki/Gate_Control "Gate Control") closes the gate, killing several pilots. Cassian contacts Bodhi and asks him to contact the fleet to attempt to open the gate so they can transmit the plans. Bohdi asks the ground troops to find a master switch so he can communicate with the fleet by interfacing with the communications tower.

Rebel troops land from the gunship to reinforce Rogue One. The fleet begins to attack the Shield Gate but to no avail. Rebel X-wings engage numerous [TIE fighters](/wiki/TIE/ln_space_superiority_starfighter "TIE/ln space superiority starfighter") stationed on the Shield Gate, with both sides suffering substantial casualties. Jyn finds the plans on the Citadel mainframe — codenamed [*Stardust*](/wiki/Death_Star_plans "Death Star plans"), in which Jyn immediately recognizes the name as a secret personal message from her father to help her find the Death Star plans. K-2SO closes the vault door moments before stormtroopers arrive to investigate. K-2SO desperately attempts to lure them away, but the stormtroopers become suspicious and he is forced to attack them. Before being destroyed by enemy fire, K-2SO locks the vault door so the stormtroopers could not open it again, allowing time for his comrades to retrieve the plans. Krennic is informed that the vault has had unauthorized access and goes to investigate. Jyn and Cassian climb the data vault and physically remove the data plans. Right after the retrieval of the plans, however, the duo are ambushed by Krennic. He shoots Cassian with his blaster, causing him to fall.

Chirrut is killed after activating the master switch to allow communication with the Rebel fleet from Rook's shuttle. A squadron of [Y-wings](/wiki/BTL-A4_Y-wing_assault_starfighter/bomber "BTL-A4 Y-wing assault starfighter/bomber") commanded by [Jon Vander](/wiki/Jon_Vander "Jon Vander") launches multiple ion torpedoes at a Star Destroyer, disabling it.

Rook manages to contact Raddus' flagship, the [MC75 Star Cruiser](/wiki/MC75_Star_Cruiser "MC75 Star Cruiser") *[Profundity](/wiki/Profundity "Profundity")*, and informs them they must open the deflector shield to allow the Death Star plans to be transmitted to them. Shortly after, a [thermal imploder](/wiki/Thermal_imploder "Thermal imploder") was thrown into his ship, killing him and destroying the shuttle. Having received Rook's transmission, Raddus quickly formulates a plan to break open the shield using the resources he has available.

Raddus orders a [*Sphyrna*-class Hammerhead corvette](/wiki/Sphyrna-class_Hammerhead_corvette "Sphyrna-class Hammerhead corvette"), *[Lightmaker](/wiki/Lightmaker "Lightmaker")*, to physically ram into the side of a disabled Star Destroyer, which pushes it into a second Star Destroyer close by, and creates a chain reaction that effectively destroys all three ships. Baze, having been inspired by Îmwe's sacrifice, repeats his comrade's signature phrase — "I am one with the Force, and the Force is with me" — multiple times, but is then killed by a grenade. One of the Star Destroyers then crashes into the shield gate protecting Scarif and disables the planetary shield, allowing full communications to be re-established. Krennic pursues and corners Jyn on the top of the Citadel tower but before he can kill her, Cassian, who had survived the blaster wound, shoots and badly wounds Krennic. Jyn then successfully transmits the schematics to the Rebel command ship, before helping the injured Cassian into a nearby elevator.

Tarkin arrives with the Death Star and fires a single reactor ignition of the superlaser to destroy the compromised base in an attempt to prevent the plans from falling into enemy hands. While the blast overshoots the base — though the fringes of the beam take out the transmitter, and Krennic along with it — and impacts several kilometers away, it nonetheless triggers an explosion powerful enough to guarantee the death of everyone in the vicinity. Jyn and Cassian, knowing they have no means of escape, await the approaching blast on a beach near the base. In their final moments, Cassian assures Jyn that her father would have been proud, and seconds later the blast incinerates them, along with the base.

After paying respects to his fallen comrades, Raddus orders his fleet to jump to [hyperspace](/wiki/Hyperspace "Hyperspace"), but before the entire fleet can escape, most are intercepted by Vader's Star Destroyer, *[Devastator](/wiki/Devastator "Devastator"),* which begins to either destroy or disable the blockaded Alliance ships. Vader boards Admiral Raddus' disabled command ship and singlehandedly massacres many Rebel troops in pursuit of the Death Star plans, only to watch as the [CR90 Corvette](/wiki/CR90_corvette "CR90 corvette") *[Tantive IV](/wiki/Tantive_IV "Tantive IV")* launches from the hanger bay, narrowly escaping Vader's grasp.

### Secret mission to Tatooine[]

:   "*Your Highness. Transmission we received… What is it they've sent us?"  
    "Hope.*"
:   ―Raymus Antilles and Leia Organa[[1]](#cite_note-Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story-1)

Aboard the *Tantive IV*, Princess [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") receives the stolen plans and declares that the Rebellion has just received "[hope](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope")." The *Tantive IV* jumps into hyperspace.

## Development[]

### Origins[]

:   "*I started thinking about which story would I like to see told? I informally pitched it around...One of the people I pitched it to was Pablo, and he was pretty enthusiastic about it as well...I made an appointment with Kathy and Kiri, pitched the 20-minute version of this, and got a pretty good response.*"
:   ―John Knoll[[10]](#cite_note-SWCA_Liveblog-10)

 [![Rogue One concept art revealed at Celebration Anaheim](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0b/Rogue_One_Concept_Art_Celebration.png/revision/latest?cb=20160813063754) [![Rogue One concept art revealed at Celebration Anaheim](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0b/Rogue_One_Concept_Art_Celebration.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160813063754)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0b/Rogue_One_Concept_Art_Celebration.png/revision/latest?cb=20160813063754) 

*Rogue One* concept art revealed at Celebration Anaheim

 

[John Knoll](/wiki/John_Knoll "John Knoll"), a visual effects supervisor and the chief creative officer at [ILM](/wiki/Industrial_Light_%26_Magic "Industrial Light & Magic"), began developing the idea for *Rogue One* in the mid-2000s, after learning that [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas") was developing a [*Star Wars* live-action TV series](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Underworld "Star Wars: Underworld"). However, Knoll put aside the idea once he realized that it would not fit within the show's concept.[[11]](#cite_note-CEpanel-11)[[12]](#cite_note-SW-SWCE_2016:_15_Things_We_Learned_from_the_Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story_Panel-12) The series was eventually put on indefinite hold due to budget constraints,[[13]](#cite_note-13) and Lucas decided to retire from filmmaking,[[14]](#cite_note-14) hiring [Kathleen Kennedy](/wiki/Kathleen_Kennedy "Kathleen Kennedy") as the new head of [Lucasfilm](/wiki/Lucasfilm "Lucasfilm").[[15]](#cite_note-SW-Passing_the_Baton:_Meet_Kathleen_Kennedy-15) According to Kennedy, Lucas was "really interested in exploring all the stories that existed inside the universe."[[10]](#cite_note-SWCA_Liveblog-10) (Lucas had long considered making films outside of the saga, dating back to development of the original *Star Wars* film.[[16]](#cite_note-16)) Lucasfilm settled on calling these non-episodic adventures the *[Star Wars Anthology Series](/wiki/Star_Wars_Anthology_Series "Star Wars Anthology Series")*.[[10]](#cite_note-SWCA_Liveblog-10) At the urging of his colleagues,[[11]](#cite_note-CEpanel-11) Knoll pitched his idea to various people within Lucasfilm, including [Lucasfilm Story Group](/wiki/Lucasfilm_Story_Group "Lucasfilm Story Group") member [Pablo Hidalgo](/wiki/Pablo_Hidalgo "Pablo Hidalgo"), who was enthusiastic about the idea. This led to a meeting with Kennedy and [Kiri Hart](/wiki/Kiri_Hart "Kiri Hart"), a member of the Story Group and Lucasfilm's vice president of development. Kennedy, who said she was president "for about 10 minutes" when she had the discussion with Knoll, thought it was a great idea and that "there was no way" she could say no to the idea. Like Kennedy, Hart was "immediately excited about" the film.[[10]](#cite_note-SWCA_Liveblog-10) It was then chosen as the first stand-alone film to be produced, due to the involvement of plot elements that general audiences would be familiar with.[[17]](#cite_note-17)

### Production[]

:   "*Gary Whitta did the first draft and then I came in and did a couple of drafts and then after me came Tony Gilroy, Christopher McQuarrie, Scott Burns, I believe David Arndt had some notes on it, and then Tony Gilroy came back on again. And it's astonishing to me that, for me, from my point of view, how well it turned out, given how many writers were working on it any one time.*"
:   ―[Chris Weitz](/wiki/Chris_Weitz "Chris Weitz")[[18]](#cite_note-McQuarrie-18)

[Gary Whitta](/wiki/Gary_Whitta "Gary Whitta"), who had written [*The Book of Eli*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Book_of_Eli "wikipedia:The Book of Eli") and [*After Earth*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/After_Earth "wikipedia:After Earth"), was hired to write the film's screenplay.[[3]](#cite_note-Director_Announced-3) The main characters did not die in the original script, due to the filmmakers' assumption that Disney would want to use the characters again.[[19]](#cite_note-19) Whitta's script also ended with a wedding.[[20]](#cite_note-Earlier_Scripts-20) On [March 12](/wiki/March_12 "March 12"), [2015](/wiki/2015 "2015"), it was announced that [Chris Weitz](/wiki/Chris_Weitz "Chris Weitz") would take over screenwriting duties from Whitta.[[21]](#cite_note-First_Stand-Alone-21) (Reportedly, [Scott Z. Burns](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scott_Z._Burns "wikipedia:Scott Z. Burns") and [Christopher McQuarrie](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christopher_McQuarrie "wikipedia:Christopher McQuarrie") also wrote drafts of the script.[[22]](#cite_note-22)[[23]](#cite_note-23)[[24]](#cite_note-true_and_false-24)[[18]](#cite_note-McQuarrie-18)) It was further announced that the film would be titled *Rogue One*[[21]](#cite_note-First_Stand-Alone-21)—a name coined by Whitta during the writing process[[25]](#cite_note-Whitta_Title-25)—and that [Felicity Jones](/wiki/Felicity_Jones "Felicity Jones"), who had been nominated for an Academy Award for her performance in [*The Theory of Everything*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Theory_of_Everything_(2014_film) "wikipedia:The Theory of Everything (2014 film)"), had been cast in the film.[[21]](#cite_note-First_Stand-Alone-21) In Weitz's draft, it was not made clear that the Empire was building the [Death Star](/wiki/Death_Star "Death Star"): "It was just the sense that the rebellion — that something bad was going down and we need to find out about it. There was this developing sense of dread throughout the film."[[20]](#cite_note-Earlier_Scripts-20)

John Knoll wanted the film to be shot on a low budget, going so far as to propose that some sets be reused from [*The Force Awakens*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VII_The_Force_Awakens "Star Wars: Episode VII The Force Awakens").[[26]](#cite_note-The_Art_of_Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story-26) However, "As we got into more detailed story development, you know, the canvas sort of kept expanding and more epic things kept popping up and going into the movie. And you know, the discussion with Disney, it became clear that they were really open to the idea of going bigger with these movies."[[27]](#cite_note-27) [Gareth Edwards](/wiki/Gareth_Edwards "Gareth Edwards"), who had directed [*Monsters*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Monsters_(2010_film) "wikipedia:Monsters (2010 film)") and was directing [*Godzilla*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Godzilla_(2014_film) "wikipedia:Godzilla (2014 film)") at the time, was hired to direct the film,[[3]](#cite_note-Director_Announced-3) early in the creative process.[[10]](#cite_note-SWCA_Liveblog-10) A [previsualization](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Previsualization "wikipedia:Previsualization") reel based on the story was created using footage from many other films, such as [*WarGames*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/WarGames "wikipedia:WarGames"), [*Aliens*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aliens_(film) "wikipedia:Aliens (film)"), and [*Zero Dark Thirty*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zero_Dark_Thirty_(film) "wikipedia:Zero Dark Thirty (film)").[[28]](#cite_note-28)[[29]](#cite_note-29) Edwards also used [ILM's](/wiki/Industrial_Light_%26_Magic "Industrial Light & Magic") new developments in [virtual reality](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Virtual_reality "wikipedia:Virtual reality") to aid in pre-visualizing the film.[[30]](#cite_note-30)

The film began principal photography in [London](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/London "wikipedia:London") in [August](/wiki/August "August") 2015. This was announced during the [D23 Expo](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Disney_D23 "wikipedia:Disney D23") that same month. Additionally, a [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") blog post revealed the full cast for the film.[[31]](#cite_note-Cast_and_Crew_Announced-31) At least two of the cast underwent special training for their roles: Felicity Jones in a style of martial arts and [Diego Luna](/wiki/Diego_Luna "Diego Luna") in military training.[[8]](#cite_note-NYT-8)[[32]](#cite_note-GMALuna-32) Members of the [British Armed Forces](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_Armed_Forces "wikipedia:British Armed Forces") were also hired as extras.[[33]](#cite_note-33) The production team worked to create a film that felt real, as if it was taking place in a real location; and one that was set within the gray areas of Star Wars, as opposed to the clear morality of the [original *Star Wars* trilogy](/wiki/Original_trilogy "Original trilogy").[[10]](#cite_note-SWCA_Liveblog-10) The look of the film was inspired by the work of artist [Frederic Remington](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frederic_Remington "wikipedia:Frederic Remington"),[[34]](#cite_note-34) as well as footage of real-life wars.[[35]](#cite_note-EdwardsReshoots-35) [Warwick Davis](/wiki/Warwick_Davis "Warwick Davis"), who had a small role in the film, described Edwards' directing style: "He would shoot in a very unique way where stuff was kind of almost improvised, but you never knew quite when he was shooting and when he wasn't, so you just kept doing stuff just in case he was rolling at that time."[[36]](#cite_note-36)

Certain *Star Wars* traditions were eschewed in post-production, such as an opening crawl (though one was included in Whitta's original script) and "wipe" scene transitions.[[37]](#cite_note-37) ILM utilized unused footage from *A New Hope* to insert Rebel pilots from that film into *Rogue One*; Edwards had the idea after stumbling across a box of negatives while touring the [Lucasfilm Archives](/wiki/Lucasfilm_Archives "Lucasfilm Archives").[[38]](#cite_note-38)

### Reshoots[]

:   "*And they were in such a swamp... they were in so much terrible, terrible trouble that all you could do was improve their position.*"
:   ―[Tony Gilroy](/wiki/Tony_Gilroy "Tony Gilroy"), on the film's reshoots[[39]](#cite_note-HWR-39)

Initial plans for reshoots had already been made upon the film's conception. According to Edwards, "it was always part of the plan to do reshoots. We always knew we were coming back somewhere to do stuff. We just didn't know what it would be until we started sculpting the film in the edit."[[40]](#cite_note-40) However, in June 2016, rumors surfaced that Disney had ordered substantial reshoots in an effort to "lighten" the film's tone,[[41]](#cite_note-41)[[42]](#cite_note-42) with [Tony Gilroy](/wiki/Tony_Gilroy "Tony Gilroy") and [Simon Crane](/wiki/Simon_Crane "Simon Crane") having been hired to assist.[[43]](#cite_note-Simon_Crane-43)[[44]](#cite_note-44)[[24]](#cite_note-true_and_false-24)

In truth, after Edwards had delivered his final cut of the film, Gilroy had been hired to write, shoot and edit new material,[[39]](#cite_note-HWR-39) for which he was paid over $5 million.[[45]](#cite_note-45) Edwards attributed the lengthy reshoots to the spontaneous, [cinéma vérité](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cin%C3%A9ma_v%C3%A9rit%C3%A9 "wikipedia:Cinéma vérité") nature of the production.[[35]](#cite_note-EdwardsReshoots-35) According to *Entertainment Weekly*, the reshoots dealt more with character development rather than the plotline. As explained by Kathleen Kennedy, "There's nothing about the story that's changing, with a few things that we're picking up in additional photography. I think that's the most important thing, to reassure fans that it's the movie we intended to make."[[24]](#cite_note-true_and_false-24) The script underwent structural changes, with (among other things) all character deaths moved toward the end, and the addition of the Darth Vader ending sequence.[[20]](#cite_note-Earlier_Scripts-20)

Gilroy later described his role as that of a "fixer," in which he needed to come in like a doctor who could not afford to be emotionally attached to critically injured patient.[[46]](#cite_note-TimesUnion-46) In [2025](/wiki/2025 "2025"), Gilroy, much like Edwards and Chris Weitz, affirmed he had no intention of getting into the behind the scenes production of *Rogue One*, saying "I have fed my family by not talking about *Rogue One*."[[47]](#cite_note-GilroyHSC05-19-47)

### Music[]

The film's [musical score](/wiki/Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story_(soundtrack) "Rogue One: A Star Wars Story (soundtrack)") was originally composed by [Alexandre Desplat](/wiki/Alexandre_Desplat "Alexandre Desplat"), although [Michael Giacchino](/wiki/Michael_Giacchino "Michael Giacchino") took over during post-production.[[48]](#cite_note-Score2-48)

## Release and reception[]

 [![The cast announcement photo for the film](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/Rogue_One_Cast.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151218061436) [![The cast announcement photo for the film](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/Rogue_One_Cast.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/275?cb=20151218061436)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/Rogue_One_Cast.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20151218061436) 

The cast announcement photo for the film

 

A brief teaser trailer was shown for Celebration Anaheim attendees, depicting the Death Star far off in the distance on a jungle world.[[10]](#cite_note-SWCA_Liveblog-10) Lucasfilm was not able to promote the film anywhere outside of Celebration Anaheim, however, during the summer of 2015, due to the similarities between the titles of *Rogue One* and the then-upcoming film [*Mission: Impossible – Rogue Nation*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mission:_Impossible_%E2%80%93_Rogue_Nation "wikipedia:Mission: Impossible – Rogue Nation"). The title of *Rogue Nation* was registered with the Motion Picture Association of America prior to *Rogue One*, leading to the embargo on *Rogue One* promotion.[[49]](#cite_note-MI5-49) On [April 7](/wiki/April_7 "April 7"), [2016](/wiki/2016 "2016"), a teaser trailer debuted during [ABC's](/wiki/ABC_Television_Network "ABC Television Network") [*Good Morning America*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Good_Morning_America "wikipedia:Good Morning America"). A ten-second preview of the teaser had been released online the day before.[[50]](#cite_note-Teaser_preview-50) On [July 15](/wiki/July_15 "July 15"), there was a *Rogue One* panel at [Celebration Europe](/wiki/Celebration_Europe_(2016) "Celebration Europe (2016)") featuring Gareth Edwards and Kathleen Kennedy;[[51]](#cite_note-SW-Kathleen_Kennedy_and_Rogue_One_Director_Gareth_Edwards_to_Attend_Star_Wars_Celebration_Europe-51) During the panel, a featurette and a new trailer were released; The featurette aired that night during the ABC broadcast of *Secrets of the Force Awakens: A Cinematic Journey*.[[52]](#cite_note-52) A trailer aired during the [2016 Summer Olympics](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/2016_Summer_Olympics "wikipedia:2016 Summer Olympics").[[53]](#cite_note-53)

Beginning on [September 20](/wiki/September_20 "September 20"), [TNT](/wiki/Turner_Network_Television "Turner Network Television") aired the first six *Star Wars* films. This was part of a deal in which [Turner](/wiki/Turner_Entertainment "Turner Entertainment") networks received exclusive rights to air eleven *Star Wars* films, including *Rogue One* in 2019.[[54]](#cite_note-54) On [October 12](/wiki/October_12 "October 12"), it was revealed that a new trailer would be released the following day on [October 13](/wiki/October_13 "October 13").[[55]](#cite_note-Trailer_3_announcement-55) ABC aired an additional preview of the film on [November 24](/wiki/November_24 "November 24"), as part of their "Magical Holiday Celebration."[[56]](#cite_note-56) On [December 2](/wiki/December_2 "December 2"), [Twitter](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Twitter "wikipedia:Twitter") hosted a [livestream](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Livestream "wikipedia:Livestream") Q&A with Edwards and crew members;[[57]](#cite_note-57) On the same day, members of the press were invited to [Skywalker Ranch](/wiki/Skywalker_Ranch "Skywalker Ranch") to view 28 minutes of footage from the film.[[58]](#cite_note-58) Cast and crew made various media appearances, most prominently on [*Jimmy Kimmel Live!*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jimmy_Kimmel_Live! "wikipedia:Jimmy Kimmel Live!"),[[59]](#cite_note-59)[[60]](#cite_note-60) [*The Tonight Show Starring Jimmy Fallon*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Tonight_Show_Starring_Jimmy_Fallon "wikipedia:The Tonight Show Starring Jimmy Fallon"),[[61]](#cite_note-61)[[62]](#cite_note-62) *Good Morning America*,[[32]](#cite_note-GMALuna-32) [*Conan*](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Conan_(talk_show) "wikipedia:Conan (talk show)"),[[63]](#cite_note-63) [Sirius XM](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sirius_XM_Holdings "wikipedia:Sirius XM Holdings"), and [MTV News](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/MTV_News "wikipedia:MTV News").[[64]](#cite_note-64)[[65]](#cite_note-65) The film had its Hollywood premiere on [December 10](/wiki/December_10 "December 10").[[66]](#cite_note-66)

Some of the cast and crew participated in [UNICEF's](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/UNICEF "wikipedia:UNICEF") Force for Change and Kid Power programs, creating [Target](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Target_Corporation "wikipedia:Target Corporation")-exclusive T-shirts, of which five dollars from each would contribute to the cause.[[67]](#cite_note-SW-Gareth_Edwards,_Felicity_Jones,_and_More_Come_Together_for_'Force_4_Fashion'_T-Shirts-67)[[68]](#cite_note-68) Edwards also used the opportunity of making the film to promote the [ASSERT](http://angelmanuk.org) charity.[[69]](#cite_note-69) As with [*The Force Awakens*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_VII_The_Force_Awakens "Star Wars: Episode VII The Force Awakens"),[[70]](#cite_note-70) a terminally ill cancer patient—[Neil Hanvey](/wiki/Neil_Hanvey "Neil Hanvey")—was allowed to see the film early. Hanvey passed away two days after seeing the film.[[71]](#cite_note-71)

Tickets went on sale on the midnight of November 28,[[72]](#cite_note-SW-Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story_Tickets_On_Sale_Worldwide-72) followed by reports that Fandango had crashed due to high demand.[[73]](#cite_note-73)[[74]](#cite_note-74) The film had the second biggest day one pre-sales, following *The Force Awakens*.[[75]](#cite_note-75)

On [January 22](/wiki/January_22 "January 22"), [2017](/wiki/2017 "2017"), the film surpassed the one billion dollar mark for global box office receipts.[[76]](#cite_note-billion-76) On [May 17](/wiki/May_17 "May 17") of that year, the film was awarded the title of "[Movie of the Year](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/MTV_Movie_Award_for_Movie_of_the_Year "wikipedia:MTV Movie Award for Movie of the Year")" at the [MTV Movie & TV Awards](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/MTV_Movie_%26_TV_Awards "wikipedia:MTV Movie & TV Awards").[[77]](#cite_note-Empire_Turns_40-77) Regardless of how well the film performed, there were never plans for a sequel.[[78]](#cite_note-78)

In April [2020](/wiki/2020 "2020"), co-writers Chris Weitz and Gary Whitta recorded a YouTube commentary and Q&A for the film, hosted by IGN.[[79]](#cite_note-79) On [May 17](/wiki/May_17 "May 17"), [2025](/wiki/2025 "2025"), *Rogue One* was the number one most watched film on [Disney+](/wiki/Disney%2B "Disney+")[[80]](#cite_note-Most_Watched-80) after the conclusion of its prequel series, *[Andor](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Andor "Star Wars: Andor")*, on [May 13](/wiki/May_13 "May 13"), 2025.[[81]](#cite_note-Declassified-81)

## Continuity[]

 [![Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope depicts the aftermath of the battle to steal the Death Star plans.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/Devastatortantiveiv.png/revision/latest?cb=20201017104531) [![Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope depicts the aftermath of the battle to steal the Death Star plans.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/Devastatortantiveiv.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201017104531)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/02/Devastatortantiveiv.png/revision/latest?cb=20201017104531) 

*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope* depicts the aftermath of the battle to steal the Death Star plans.

 

*Rogue One* is set between the films [*Star Wars*: Episode III *Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith") and [*Star Wars*: Episode IV *A New Hope*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope"), during the [Age of the Empire](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"). The film revolves around a group of resistance fighters who unite to steal the plans to the [Death Star](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station"), the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire")'s deep space mobile [battle station](/wiki/Battle_station "Battle station") that is capable of destroying entire [planets](/wiki/Planet "Planet").[[10]](#cite_note-SWCA_Liveblog-10) The theft of the plans was first referenced in the opening crawl of *A New Hope*, which described the event as the Rebel Alliance's "first victory against the evil Galactic Empire." The crawl further states that "Rebel [spies](/wiki/Spy "Spy") managed to steal secret plans to ... the DEATH STAR". The opening scenes of *A New Hope* deal with that battle's aftermath, with [Princess](/wiki/Prince "Prince") [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo") of [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan") [fleeing](/wiki/Secret_mission_to_Tatooine "Secret mission to Tatooine") from the Empire with the plans in order to deliver them to the Rebel Alliance. The Death Star is ultimately destroyed in *A New Hope* after the princess and her companions—[Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"), [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo "Han Solo"), [Chewbacca](/wiki/Chewbacca "Chewbacca"), and the [droids](/wiki/Droid "Droid") [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2") and [C-3PO](/wiki/C-3PO "C-3PO")—deliver the plans to the Rebellion and a weakness in the station is discovered.[[82]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-82)

The title *Rogue One* refers to a [callsign](/wiki/Callsign "Callsign"), but is also intended as a pun, as the film is the first canon live-action film that is not part of the saga and is, therefore, the "rogue" one.[[83]](#cite_note-titlemeaning-83) Unlike the previous films, *Rogue One* does not revolve around the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi"). Rather, the film is about a group of people who do not have the ability to use [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force") and have to find a way to bring hope to a [galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy") ruled by the Empire. Also unlike the [original trilogy](/wiki/Original_trilogy "Original trilogy"), which provided a black and white view of good and evil, Edwards stated at [Celebration Anaheim](/wiki/Celebration_Anaheim_(2015) "Celebration Anaheim (2015)") that *Rogue One* "is gray" and that the film could be described as "Real…This is a real place that we're really in…"[[10]](#cite_note-SWCA_Liveblog-10)

## Adaptations and tie-in media[]

The *Rogue One* merchandise line officially launched on [September 30](/wiki/September_30 "September 30"), 2016.[[84]](#cite_note-SW-SWCE_2016:_First_Rogue_One_Action_Figure_Revealed-84) A prequel comic miniseries of the film was set to be released in [October](/wiki/October "October") and published by [Marvel Comics](/wiki/Marvel_Comics "Marvel Comics"), containing three issues and a one-shot,[[85]](#cite_note-Rogue_One_prequel_comic-85) until it was revealed that the miniseries has been canceled on [May 17](/wiki/May_17 "May 17").[[86]](#cite_note-Comic_cancelation-86) Two of the movie's other related products were also canceled before they were released: *Rogue One: A Star Wars Story: Rebel Alliance Field Manual*,[[87]](#cite_note-Field_Manual-87) which was canceled when the publisher [Media Lab Books](/wiki/Media_Lab_Publishing "Media Lab Publishing") lost the license,[[88]](#cite_note-JB_Twitter-88) and *Rogue One: A Star Wars Story: The Official Visual Story Guide*.[[89]](#cite_note-Edelweiss_Visual_Story_Guide-89) On [November 15](/wiki/November_15 "November 15"), [Del Rey](/wiki/Del_Rey "Del Rey") published a prequel novel to the film, entitled *[Catalyst: A Rogue One Novel](/wiki/Catalyst:_A_Rogue_One_Novel "Catalyst: A Rogue One Novel")*.[[90]](#cite_note-Catalyst_Amazon-90) [Dorling Kindersley](/wiki/Dorling_Kindersley "Dorling Kindersley") released an [art book](/wiki/The_Art_of_Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story "The Art of Rogue One: A Star Wars Story") and [ultimate visual guide](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Rogue_One:_The_Ultimate_Visual_Guide "Star Wars: Rogue One: The Ultimate Visual Guide") for the film on [December 16](/wiki/December_16 "December 16"), the same day as the release of the film itself.[[91]](#cite_note-amazonart-91)[[92]](#cite_note-amazonvisual-92) A short story titled "[The Voice of the Empire](/wiki/The_Voice_of_the_Empire "The Voice of the Empire")" tying into the film was featured in [*Star Wars Insider* 170](/wiki/Star_Wars_Insider_170 "Star Wars Insider 170").[[93]](#cite_note-SWCE-93) A *Rogue One* expansion was released for the video game *[Star Wars Battlefront](/wiki/Star_Wars_Battlefront "Star Wars Battlefront")*.[[94]](#cite_note-SW-<i-94)[[95]](#cite_note-EA-Rogue_One:_Scarif-95) *[Star Wars: Galaxy of Heroes](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galaxy_of_Heroes "Star Wars: Galaxy of Heroes")* hosted several exclusive events introducing characters from *Rogue One*.[[96]](#cite_note-swgof-96)

In August 2016, Lucasfilm released a series of online images advertising [Hasbro](/wiki/Hasbro "Hasbro")'s *Rogue One* toy line, which debuted on September 30.[[97]](#cite_note-97) The toys were also featured in *Go Rogue*, an officially sponsored, fan-created online video series that continued throughout September.[[98]](#cite_note-SW-Go_Rogue_Contest_Winners-98)[[99]](#cite_note-Star_Wars_Show_Rogue_One_Droid-99) The [Black Series](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Black_Series "Star Wars: The Black Series") figure of Jyn Erso was released on [October 15](/wiki/October_15 "October 15"), 2016. By [September 4](/wiki/September_4 "September 4"), 2016, the figure had already skyrocketed to become the #1 Best Seller in Amazon's Action & Toy Figures category, based on hourly-updated figures.[[100]](#cite_note-amazonbseriesjyn-100)[[101]](#cite_note-ersofigureimage-101) [Verizon](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Verizon_Communications "wikipedia:Verizon Communications") sponsored [*Rogue One: Recon*](/wiki/Rogue_One:_Recon_A_Star_Wars_360_Experience "Rogue One: Recon A Star Wars 360 Experience"), a 3D experience created by [ILM Experience Lab](/wiki/ILM_Immersive "ILM Immersive").[[102]](#cite_note-SW-ILMxLAB's_Mark_Miller_on_Rogue_One:_Recon_and_Putting_Fans_in_X-wings-102) [Nissan](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nissan "wikipedia:Nissan") offered a *Rogue One*–themed Limited Edition of its 2017 [Nissan Rogue](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Nissan_Rogue "wikipedia:Nissan Rogue").[[103]](#cite_note-103) In October 2016, *Rogue One*–inspired commercials aired for [Duracell](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Duracell "wikipedia:Duracell"), Nissan and [Gilette](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gillette_(brand) "wikipedia:Gillette (brand)") products.[[104]](#cite_note-104)[[105]](#cite_note-105)[[106]](#cite_note-106)

### Home media[]

*Rogue One* became available on Digital HD on [March 24](/wiki/March_24 "March 24"), 2017, and on Blu-ray and DVD on [April 4](/wiki/April_4 "April 4"), 2017. The retail version contains bonuses exclusive to the store outlet where it was purchased. Target's 5-disc set includes collectible packaging with interchangeable character covers and exclusive bonus content (Blu-ray 3D + two Blu-ray + DVD + DVD exclusive content – 2 additional bonus features + Digital HD + collectible packaging), Best Buy has a 4-disc set with exclusive SteelBook packaging (Blu-ray 3D + two Blu-ray + DVD + Digital HD + SteelBook packaging), and Wal-Mart sells a 3-disc set with exclusive K-2SO packaging and two Galactic Connexions trading discs (two Blu-ray + DVD + Digital HD + K-2SO packaging + two Galactic Connexions trading discs). In addition to the film itself, the various home-media releases include various special content, including John Knoll's inspiration for the concept of the film, coverage of the cast regarding their respective characters, coverage of [easter eggs](/wiki/Easter_egg_(virtual) "Easter egg (virtual)") hidden throughout the film, and behind-the-scenes looks at how Tarkin and Leia were given digital touchups.[[107]](#cite_note-SW-The_Mission_Comes_Home:_Rogue_One:_A_Star_Wars_Story_Arrives_Soon_on_Digital_HD_and_Blu-ray-107)

### Cover gallery[]
